`requiredWorkers` callers succeed; everyone else gets a clean 409 instead\n// of silently over-filling the 
booking.\nconst handleAutoBookAccept = async (req, res, booking) => {\n  try {\n    const workerId =

'$acceptedWorkers' }, '$requiredWorkers'] },\n      },\n      {\n        $push: { acceptedWorkers: workerId },\n

{\n      return res.status(409).json({\n        success: false,\n        message: 'This request has just been filled 
by other workers. Better luck next time!',\n      });\n    }\n\n    let finalBooking = updated;\n    const isFulfilled
